	####################################################################
formable_nations_africa_category  = {
	formable_nations_africa  = {#continent
		
		ai_will_do  = {
			factor  = 1
			modifier  = {
				factor  = 0
				has_global_flag  = ai_disabled
			}
		}
		
		cost  = 0  days_re_enable  = 0
		
		visible  = {
			NOT  = { has_country_flag  = unform_available }
			NOT  = { has_country_flag  = hide_formable_nations }
			OR  = {
				
				capital_scope  = { is_on_continent  = africa }
			}
		}
		
		available  = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip  = { 
				tooltip  = africa_requirement_tooltip 
				OR  = {
					AND  = {
						all_state  = {
							OR  = {
								AND  = {
									is_on_continent  = africa
									NOT  = {
										OR  = {
											state  = 697
											state  = 178
											state  = 702
											state  = 703
											state  = 704
											state  = 297
											state  = 705
											state  = 708
											state  = 709
											state  = 706
											state  = 707
											state  = 713
											state  = 543
											state  = 906
										}
									}
									is_controlled_by  = ROOT
								}
								NOT  = { is_on_continent  = africa }
								state  = 697
								state  = 178
								state  = 702
								state  = 703
								state  = 704
								state  = 297
								state  = 705
								state  = 708
								state  = 709
								state  = 706
								state  = 707
								state  = 713
								state  = 543
								state  = 906
							}
						}
					}
					AND  = {
						is_ai  = no
						has_global_flag  = debug_mode
					}
				}
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip  = { tooltip  = not_already_existing_tt NOT  = { any_country  = { has_cosmetic_tag  = FORM_AFR } } }
			custom_trigger_tooltip   = { tooltip  = is_puppet_tooltip OR  = { is_subject  = no has_global_flag  = puppets_allowed } }
		}
		icon  = formable_nations_africa
		complete_effect  = { capital_scope  = { set_state_flag  = formable_nations_old_capital }
			set_cosmetic_tag  = FORM_AFR
			add_stability  = 0.2
			add_ideas  = generic_recent_political_unification
            add_ideas  = generic_recent_army_unification
            add_ideas  = generic_recent_economic_unification	
			custom_effect_tooltip  = core_land
			hidden_effect  = { sound_effect  = complete_focus  set_country_flag  = unform_available
				every_state  = {
					limit  = { 
						is_on_continent  = africa
						NOT  = { is_core_of  = ROOT }
					}
					add_core_of  = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

		ai_will_do  = {
			factor  = 1
			modifier  = {
				factor  = 0
				has_global_flag  = ai_disabled 
			}
		}
		
		cost  = 0  days_re_enable  = 0
		
		visible  = {
			NOT  = { has_country_flag  = unform_available }
			NOT  = { has_country_flag  = hide_formable_nations }

				capital_scope  = { is_on_continent  = south_america }
			}
		}
		
		available  = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip  = { 
				tooltip  = south_america_requirement_tooltip

									state  = 690
									state  = 693

									state  = 318
									state  = 319
									state  = 692
									state  = 694
									state  = 308
									state  = 686

									state  = 313
									state  = 312
									state  = 314
									state  = 316
									state  = 317
									state  = 299
									state  = 720
									state  = 649
								}
							}
							NOT  = {
								is_on_continent  = south_america
							}
							OR  = {
								state  = 690
								state  = 693
								state  = 689

								state  = 692
